<text>Wonderful info center for Mono Lake. Find out about its ecology, geology and about the water politics of California. It's also a book shop and a shop of very tasteful gifts.  And staffed by knowledgeable and friendly staff.

Mono lake is an invaluable part of the north south American by way for migratory birds, close to being completely destroyed by LA's thirst. But an agreement was made in 1994 that gave the lake some hope of stabilization and possible future restoration.<//text><rate>5<//rate><pictures>None</pictures>< UserId.>

< Review>
I absolutely love which Wich. When they say Superior sandwiches they arn't kidding. I love to get the turkey spinach wrap with a ton of veggies and red pepper and yellow mustard... Yum yum.

However this location specifically has some problems, the food is fantastic but the customer service is complete garbage.

When I go in the staff are never smiling, they never appear to be happy at their jobs. There's been a couple times where my sandwich has been clearly half-assed when they've been making it. The ingredients are falling out of a sandwich when I'm trying to open the paper wrap it's in even when I don't have that many ingredients in the sandwich in the first place.

When I've done delivery, they've gotten my order wrong quite a couple of times, making mistakes like adding cheese (I'm lactose intolerant) or even sometimes having an entirely different meat inside the sandwich or Salad that I order.

And also the time when I went to get a sandwich and they shut down 30 minutes early specifically so they could feed their family that came to visit.

While I highly recommend Which Wich, I can't exactly recommend this location. Long story short, they've gotten lazy and are kind of giving the Which Wich franchise a bad name.

still, I do find it funny that the worst which which I've ever been to is still better than any Subway I've ever been to.</Review>

<Review>I eat sandwiches every single day for lunch. Unfortunately, I cannot recommend Which Which. First, I feel like they have an overly complicated ordering process. You have to check off ingredients you want on a paper bag, then had it to an employee, who will hand it to someone else to begin making your sandwich. While inefficient I could live with that, but the mother of all sins--their bread is hard. It just tastes stale to me, and I'm a sourdough die hard. With so many better Sandwich options nearby, I definitely rate Which Which a 'Skip It.'<//Review><gmap_id>0x80c2b14c621c73c7:0x47583a0a43f5b1a3<//gmap_id>< name>
